{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+U\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Sess\+Estab\+MM (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+C\+O\+O\+K\+IE}]{z\+Cookie,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Subject,  }\item[{Z\+V\+O\+ID $\ast$}]{p\+Data,  }\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Data\+Size,  }\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Msg\+Type,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Uri,  }\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT $\ast$}]{pi\+Msg\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Establishing message session with one participant with the frist muti-\/media message in invite. 

If IM establishing successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__cb_8h_a574ebbdacbf10755def7f2eb2a38b4fc}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Cb\+Set\+Sess\+Acpted}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__cb_8h_a89ee9f1ae7c7dadf622eae7cb595f0f1}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Cb\+Set\+Sess\+Rejected}}.

While receiving message session invitation, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__cb_8h_adde287d3fda1e3f8e7f0bf539e0c03c6}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Cb\+Set\+Sess\+Recv\+IvtM}}.

While session participant has updated, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__cb_8h_a15355de691286674c44d8c1082bab417}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Cb\+Set\+Sess\+Partp\+Upted}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Sess\+Get\+Orig\+Id\+Partp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Sess\+Id,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$$\ast$}]{ppc\+Name,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$$\ast$}]{ppc\+Uri }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get original identity of participant U\+RI from message session. 

The participant is the session initiator who initialized this message session. It will return local U\+RI if local client is the session initiator. It will return identity uri if session invitation has P-\/\+Asserted-\/\+Identity information.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The session id. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em ppc\+Name} & The participant name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em ppc\+Uri} & The participant U\+RI.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The caller must copy out parameter, then use.


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Z\+OK} & Get original participant successfully. \\
\hline
{\em Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & Get original participant failed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_ImSessMsgSend()}{Mtc\_ImSessMsgSend()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+U\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Sess\+Msg\+Send (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Sess\+Id,  }\item[{Z\+C\+O\+O\+K\+IE}]{z\+Cookie,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Msg,  }\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Msg\+Type,  }\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+At\+Partp\+Lst\+Id,  }\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+At\+Type,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Font\+Info,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Traf\+Type,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Re\+Imdn\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



M\+TC Sending a message through message session. 

If IM sent message successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__cb_8h_a7346a0e2ac38993a50c5097a29fe4d12}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Cb\+Set\+Sess\+Msg\+Send\+Ok}}.

If IM sent message failed, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__cb_8h_a9bf8413f2f35510c87ef22f0ba0e455f}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Cb\+Set\+Sess\+Msg\+Send\+Failed}}.

While receiving message, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__cb_8h_a69f0bca4dcde585664541337dfa39c6a}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Cb\+Set\+Sess\+Msg\+Recv\+Msg}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The session id. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em z\+Cookie} & The user cookie. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Msg} & The message body. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Msg\+Type} & The message type, see \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__sess_8h_a34cd8378e79ec81b2f671c27ec7c7a85}{E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+I\+M\+\_\+\+S\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+At\+Partp\+Lst\+Id} & The participant list id which be mentioned. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+At\+Type} & The at function type, see \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__sess_8h_a32847b570c0721ce1aa6307cb6eec4d2}{E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+I\+M\+\_\+\+S\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+A\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Traf\+Type} & The Traffic identification, see @\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Sess\+Msg\+Get\+Traffic\+Type. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Font\+Info} & The font information. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Re\+Imdn\+Id} & The resend imdn message id. ~\newline
\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The session message id when send a message successfully, otherwise return Z\+M\+A\+X\+U\+I\+NT. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Sess\+Msg\+Send\+Geo\+Both (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Sess\+Id,  }\item[{Z\+C\+O\+O\+K\+IE}]{z\+Cookie,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Free\+Text,  }\item[{Z\+D\+O\+U\+B\+LE}]{d\+Latitude,  }\item[{Z\+D\+O\+U\+B\+LE}]{d\+Longitude,  }\item[{Z\+F\+L\+O\+AT}]{f\+Radius,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Label,  }\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Msg\+Type,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Re\+Imdn\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



mtcf M\+TC Send geolocation both free text and coordinate through session. 

If IM sent message successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__cb_8h_a7346a0e2ac38993a50c5097a29fe4d12}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Cb\+Set\+Sess\+Msg\+Send\+Ok}}.

If IM sent message failed, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__cb_8h_a9bf8413f2f35510c87ef22f0ba0e455f}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Cb\+Set\+Sess\+Msg\+Send\+Failed}}.

While receiving message, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__cb_8h_a69f0bca4dcde585664541337dfa39c6a}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Cb\+Set\+Sess\+Msg\+Recv\+Msg}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The session id. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em z\+Cookie} & The user cookie. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Free\+Text} & The free text. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em d\+Latitude} & The latitude of user place. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em d\+Longitude} & The longitude of user place. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em f\+Radius} & The radius of user place. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Label} & The label string, if Z\+N\+U\+LL indicate user\textquotesingle{}s own position, else other position. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Msg\+Type} & The message type, see \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__sess_8h_a34cd8378e79ec81b2f671c27ec7c7a85}{E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+I\+M\+\_\+\+S\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Re\+Imdn\+Id} & The resend imdn message id.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Note\+: if radius value is equal to 0, the coordinate is a point, if radius value is bigger than 0, the coordinate is a circle.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The session message id when send a message successfully, otherwise return Z\+M\+A\+X\+U\+I\+NT. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
